                        <div data-reactid="702">
                         Situated in the heart of Downtown Laurel, MS, and overlooking Central Avenue. It is old and historic, has a cozy atmosphere with wood floors and original beaded 16' ceilings. The Bed and Breakfast is located above Sweet Somethings Bakery and within the city of the new HGTV special "HOMETOWN" with Ben and Erin Napier. You are within walking distance of fabulous dining and personal shopping and the Amtrack is only 3 blocks away. Perfect for in between stops.

                        <div data-reactid="1924">
                         Covey Run Guest Lodge is conveniently located a mile off I - 20/59, Exit 17 in Livingston, AL. It is a beautiful gated country home situated on 400 acres of rolling black belt prairie. The house is approximately 3 miles from the beautiful, historic University of West AL campus. It is a great venue for parties or events such as graduation and football games. The home is very modern, while exemplifying the rural lifestyle. Guided horseback rides and fishing may be provided upon request.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1925">
                         The house is equipped with a very large kitchen that opens up into the living room. Situated with plenty of seating for bigger parties. A 50in flat screen is mounted above the fire place. Hosting the premium Dish package. The master bedroom is located downstairs, featuring a Jacuzzi and shower. The dining room, located next to the kitchen, is ideal for family style dinners. The upstairs has 4 bedrooms and 2 full baths with a large outdoor balcony. Guest are welcome to the washer and dryer and any other amenities at their convenience. The back porch and pool area are ideal for social gatherings. Whether that be just a person and their dog or a bunch of friends looking to catch up. The porch is covered and supplied with scenery that one is sure to get lost in. Off the back of the swimming pool, lies a rather large deck. Suitable for an array of activities. Covey Run's outside setting is centered around the relaxation of country living.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1926">
                         Covey Run is very unique in the sense of being able to stay in the country, while still having quick access to modern life. The house is located approximately half a mile off a paved road, while only being about a 3 minute drive to the nearest gas station. The nights are sure to serenade you with a mixture of crickets and an occasional "moo" from a cow.
                        </div>

For anyone who visits who plays the piano, there is an upright piano that actually isn't half bad! There is wifi, and the Direct TV gets plenty of channels. I went prepared with groceries and all necessities, and did not leave - nor WANT to - for three days! But I think it is only a few short miles to the city of Livingston / shopping, if need be. And for anyone visiting Tuscaloosa, it is a very easy hour's drive on the interstate. Last, but not least, the host/manager, Daniel, was EXCELLENT. To be new to airbnb, he is a PRO! He made sure I wanted for nothing, even offering to pick up anything I may have forgotten while he was running errands in town. He was accommodating, helpful, so interesting (read about his background on the site!), and it was clear that my satisfaction was his goal. I was SO satisfied, I am already coming up with a reason to book another trip! If you read my other reviews on airbnb, you may note they are all good. That is because I only review places / hosts I think are above average (choosing to stay quiet about ones which are not, and maybe giving private feedback, or usually, just not going back). This one is spectacular, and deserves far more than 5 stars. </p><span data-reactid="1930">Laurie</span><span data-reactid="1931">2016-11-26T00:00:00Z</span></li>
